td-module-title\"><a href=\"https://www.americanbluesscene.com/2017/04/linda-hopkins-dead-92/\" rel=\"bookmark\" title=\"Linda Hopkins Dead at 92\">Linda Hopkins Dead at 92</a></h3>\n\n            <div class=\"td-module-meta-info\">\n                <span class=\"td-post-author-name\"><a href=\"https://www.americanbluesscene.com/author/jdnash/\">JD Nash</a> <span>-</span> </span>                <span class=\"td-post-date\"><time class=\"entry-date updated td-module-date\" datetime=\"2017-04-12T15:30:56+00:00\">April 12, 2017</time></span>                <div class=\"td-module-comments\"><a href=\"https://www.americanbluesscene.com/2017/04/linda-hopkins-dead-92/#respond\">0</a></div>            </div>\n\n\n            <div class=\"td-excerpt\">\n                In her nearly 70 year career, she traveled the world, performed on stage, in films, and television, and released 5 albums of blues and gospel music, not including the many singles she released in the 50s and 60s.
